		id = CSA_second_convention

		available = {
			has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag

		}

		}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus CSA_second_convention"
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT =  {

							has_country_flag = CSA_social_patriot_victory

						}
					}	
				}
				country_event = { id = csa.1 days = 4 }
			}
			else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CSA_social_patriot_victory
			}

			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CSA_capone_acw_flag
				}
				country_event = { id = csa.3000 days = 4 }
			}

				#let's fire allll the flavour events

				country_event = { id = csa.76 days = 90 random = 10 }
